One of my favorite restaurants in DTLA. The restaurant is classy, beautiful and spacious. I love the high ceilings and the open kitchen. They also have a pizza station in the back where you can see the pizza being made and baked in the huge oven.
When you walk in you see the beautiful display of macaroons and desserts. Variety of gift items on the wall shelves. All the desserts are picture perfect creations. They taste heavenly and are surprisingly priced reasonably. So many flavors of macaroons to chose from and the beautiful boxes they come in. Great for gifts or just to spoil yourself.
The dining area gets very busy and loud. But the delicious food they serve makes up for that. The Margherita pizza is a must for me when I'm here. So delicious and flavorful. The Caesar salad is another must have. All the dishes I tried so far have been delicious.
The service is always good, starting from the host to the busboy, they make you feel welcomed and special. Very polite and friendly staff.
Overall a great place to eat and celebrate special occasions.

Sweet Tooth: On Saturday after dinner & dessert in DTLA, my friends took me to one of my favorite places, Bottega Louie, for more dessert to go! Yum! Bottega Louie is a beautiful & elegant restaurant, even has a museum-like pristine vibe. Love the lighting as well. The bakery section reminds me of a glossy boutique!

Awe-Inspiring: The love, creativity & dedication that goes into making each & every colorful & edible creation of Bottega Louie's dessert rocks my entire world & shines in every single bite! It often takes a while to decide on which sweet treat to select, because everything is so beautiful, often shiny & even styled with gorgeous flowers!

Play It Again, Sam: While I have tried & enjoyed each dessert I've tried, my favorite continues to be the Raspberry-filled Grand Macaron, full-on yum! Since it was no longer available, as we arrived late night, I selected a slice of the shiny red Raspberry Chocolate Cake, which was yummy as well.

Food Memories/Larger Le Grand Macaron: Please bring back! It's the size of a cake! It was love at first sight & bite when one of my friends gifted me Le Grand Raspberry Macaron during the Christmas holidays in 2015. Family had flown in & friends had arrived for a feast & to play the White Elephant game!

Hide & Seek: The moment I took a forkful of the oversized Raspberry Le Grand Macaron, with the raspberries & fluffy crème inside, I knew at once that I had to hide it (And I did!), because it would be gone in 60 seconds! Haha! It's been love ever since...until I no longer saw it on the menu...

Overall: The dessert is a must!! I love the Margherita Pizza & Portobello Fries as well & it's always fun selecting one of the colorful macarons, as the flavors are plentiful! Love the entire experience with every visit to Bottega Louie! Still dreaming of the return of the Larger Raspberry Le Grand Macaron...!

This is one of the many times I've visited this restaurant. Typically, I come here to get macaroons when visiting Cali.

Ambiance: This restaurant is massive! There is a louder talking level and very soft music playing. There is so much going on in the restaurant: full bar, restaurant, coffee bar, and a dessert area. The environment is very lively and aesthetic to the eye.

Service: I ordered my desserts at the register and the workers are not that knowledgeable about the desserts they are selling. I tried asking for suggestions and they could not explain to me the desserts they suggested.

Seating: There is plenty of seating since the place is so big! There is bar seating, table/chairs near the dessert area, and a whole restaurant area.

Celebration: This dessert looked really cute so I had to give it a try. I liked the mini vanilla macaroon that came on top of it. The dessert itself was a light vanilla pudding. with white cake and a strawberry filling. It tasted pretty good and I like how the strawberry complements the vanilla flavor.

Chocolate Raspberry: This dessert did not taste good at all! It was a really rich dark chocolate flavor with a almost sour raspberry flavor inside. I could not eat more than one bite as the dark chocolate was too overpowering.

Overall, the pastries and cakes are mediocre and overhyped. I'd say the variety of macaroons and cute packaging is the best part of coming here!

We proceeded to order the following:

Carbonara - The bucatini was a small miss. It was a bit too al dente. The flavors were pretty spot on.
Croque Madame - good choice! Very filling to say the least.

Once we got home and I unpacked, I was shocked by the fact that my cake was far from perfect... It was poorly packed or it was shaken prior to packing for pick up. I was beyond mortified! Sadly, there were no available Patisserie managers available for the weekend... Really?!?!?!?!?!?!

I wrote an email and sent in a picture right away in hopes of having someone contact me. :/

I called in and was told that I wouldn't receive a response until Monday. All I wanted was to have a perfect cake for my boyfriend's birthday! I mean let's be honest, BL cakes are not cheap!

When I called, it was even suggested that the cake moved because of poor movement on my end. I'll have you know, I made sure to not move the box at all... However, I should have checked the cake prior to leaving BL!

Fortunately for me, my sister in law helped me with the cake, so we still consumed it after we had to modify the cake in order to restore it.

Needless to say, once Monday came, I was offered a refund due to the mishap from Saturday. It was super nice of them to go above and beyond.

I do wish their Raspberry Chocolate was available in a bigger size rather than just by the slice! It would be a game changer!

Bottega Louie is truly a one stop does it all kind of location.

First - the location and ambiance is simply flat out impressive. Rather Sunday brunch or a late night dessert late in the evening there's something for everyone. The staff are amazing, delightful and knowledgeable about the menu.

But how did it taste?

Bread - unless you're starving allow it to be an accessory on your table. It's not delicious, it's cold and it's not worth the work.

Beignet's - the macaroons are life but at the end of the day their beignets are donuts. Not Café du Ma and not even close to the Grand Luxe Cafe. What I will say is that it was warm, I enjoyed the pink dusted sugar detail and the raspberry purée was amazing.

Lobster Hash - this dish is nearly a 4 star review by itself. Hash brown potatoes (fluffy not crunch) surrounded by a pool of lobster bisque under a scrambled eggs (normally poached) topped with arugula with a hefty lobster tail cascading down the side. Every bite was better than before. The only issue was that the bisque was room temp.

Sammy B.
Elite 26
Whittier, CA
22 Dessert reviews
Sep 16, 2023
10 photos
Bottega Louie feels like how it feels to walk into a Hermes or Louis Vuitton: bougie. The air is filled with energy matched with this atmosphere of excitement for the food and undeniable amounts of photos ready to be taken. The interior design is clean white with elements of gold and wood to accent such pristine decor. If they were hanging clothes next to each table and fashionable bags on the walls you would think you were dining in a Hermes or Louis Vuitton. Large windows bring in extra light along with the gaze of both the envious and curious walking by. The interior could be placed in any modern home spread or fashion magazine and it would make sense it made it there.

The service is on point. Once you get seated the waiters will come by to ask for your drinks along with giving insight to the specials and favorites of the restaurant. If you haven't done research yet you can always look around as both the Hollywood elite and the common man will have faces of excitement when the food arrives. Bottega Louie is also known for their brunches so even better if you arrived at such hours.

You cannot gain notoriety in the food world, much less Los Angeles, unless your food makes a statement and that's what Bottega Louie does: consistently delicious food done simply but with an air of classiness. But what does that actually mean? Let's dissect some food to figure that out.

Let's look at an appetizer that feels familiar but spins it in a different direction. At Bottega Louie they've created a masterpiece of food utilizing the umami flavors of a mushroom along with the familiarity of fries. The Portobello fries are large cut slices of portobello mushrooms in the shape of giant wedges. They are fried golden and topped with parsley and parmesan cheese. They come with an aioli to dip with and these things are phenomenal. Though fried the mushrooms aren't dripping in oil. Though a mushroom these won't be soggy to the bite. With the sharpness of the cheese, the creaminess of the aioli, and the earthy, almost meaty flavor of the mushroom this appetizer is highly elevated in all regards.

How about something sweet? Bottega Louie knows all about sweets but incorporates balance. The French Toast here is a must try. Using a pain de mie bread (common type of white or brown bread used in France with a soft, thin crust) these thick cut slices contain so many different flavors all telling a cohesive story. You have a slight savory flavor from the egg base, a citrus component from the fresh berries and compote, richness from the buttered sliced almonds, and the blast of sweetness from maple syrup to drizzle on the side. All different notes creating a symphony to this breakfast aria.

What of savory dishes? So many to choose from. You can have their Croque Madame, which for those who never have had one before, is like an elevated ham sandwich with a poached/over easy egg on top and béchamel sauce. The Calamari Fritti are lightly fried bouncy pieces of circular squid, a delight for both flavors and mouth feels for those who enjoy texture. And of course, the pizzas. They are phenomenal. All pizzas are cooked over an open fire in a wooden oven and you get that nice smokey flavor along with the char at the edges. They have a variety of different types ranging from the classics such as the Margherita pizza to something with more kick like the Calabrese pizza which has Calabrese salami, fennel confit, pickled Fresno chiles, fresh mozzarella, Pecorino Romano, and Malibu honey. At times they will also have speciality pizzas, for example I had one with their homemade sausage, shaved truffles, and over easy egg. It was so indulgent. Pro-tip: if you do get the pizzas let them rest when they arrive for at least five minutes. Otherwise, you'll have scorching hot breath from these fiery pizzas.

Lastly, you cannot forget the patisserie at the front of the restaurant. No reservations needed to check these well crafted pastries. Not only will each one be a visual delight but the flavors match swimmingly. They are most known for their array of different macrons and when you see them in person you'll understand why. When you buy them they have well designed boxes to wrap them in, making them a fantastic gift to someone or yourself. Rave over their glossy finishes for their cakes and the bountiful layers in their croissants.

Bottega Louie is an experience all in itself. Elevated dining is an understatement to this experience. Wrapped with the luxury of its atmosphere to the different levels of flavors it's no surprise why people from all backgrounds enjoy this restaurant. If you want to as well, make sure you bring your appetite, your camera, and a fat wallet.

See all photos from Sammy B. for Bottega Louie

I've lived in LA for over a decade and have heard positive things about Bottega Louie but never had the chance eat here until recently. Walked away pleasantly surprised!

Came in around 8:30 on a Friday without a reservation but was able to easily get a table for two. It's a huge and beautiful space with tall ceilings, chic furniture and an enticing bakery areas as soon as you walk in. This place is really nice on the eyes.

The menu is relatively simple, yet elevated Italian fare. Prices average from $20-$40 for most items and the food was elevated enough to feel like the prices were reasonably justified.

Calamari - not the best I've ever had but very well executed, classic preparation.

Truffle Arancini - could have used a little more truffle flavor but these were delicious. Definitely worth a try if you like traditional arancini and want a little twist.

Bianco Pizza - really good. Crust is crispy and airy. Toppings were on point. A little salty but all the more delicious for it.

Drinks - can't remember the names but both cocktails we tried were solid and balanced.

Overall had a really nice experience here. Wasn't the best meal I've ever had but everything was good enough for a 5 star review. Waitstaff was super attentive and friendly. Worth a try!

Reading other reviews, it seems like Bottega Louie is packed during peak hours. We ended up stopping by after visitng the Broad museum, so I believe we ate close to 3PM. The restaurant was about 25% full, and we were sat immediately.

Welcome to Hollywood. Or West Hollywood anyway. We were here for dinner and a special evening to celebrate. We were here a few days before to pick up a pretzel and some pastries. These were excellent. Now we are here for dinner.

And that was some dinner. We sat at the table and met the lovely assistant to help us through the evening. She was very helpful and friendly. We decided to start with our cocktails. A good choice at a fair price was offered. The wine was a good selection to enjoy from both Napa and over in France or Italy and more. This was brought to us along with fresh bread to try as we prepared to order. The bread was ideal. Nice and firm, but soft inside. It was very fresh. An ideal offer as we waited. We even could order two rounds of the bread which was perfect.

We made our order and then waited. The empty location then slowly filled up with more and more guests for the evening. They were all attractive and truly part of the scene. They fit the place. Knew what to eat. And how to enjoy where they were.

Our orders started with salads. These were very fresh and enjoyable. I could have made a meal from the salad by itself. It was plentiful and tasty. The arrangement was ideal. It was the "look" that made it attractive to have.

Next arrived our meals. It was a variety we selected. From a beef rid to chicken parmesan to salmon to pasta. All were different and plentiful as well.

My pasta was nice and different. Having spent several weeks in Rome in May I knew what I expected. This was nice. A bit al dente but a good sauce and fresh pasta to have. The chicken parm was a bit dry. The sauce was good. There was no side such as pasta or vegetable. It was strictly the chicken. The rib was good and tender served on mashed potatoes. The salmon was medium and had its few sides.

Deseret is a selection of pastry and macaroons. It was also very fresh and enjoyable after a graceful meal.

You are not rushed when you are here. Dinner took a few hours to enjoy as you talked and could watch the crowd there. The prices are what you expect. A dinner for 6 does cost money. So expect that to happen. This is more high-end. The service is the best.The team is excellent and proper. They do everything for you before you even expect it. They are there to help and very nice. Our comments to the managers and the team.

Bottega Louie is a wonderful place to visit. You can give it a try. It is in a wonderful area of West Hollywood. It has the right crowd. It has good food. It is a great team. And for an experience it is a place to go. As the old saying goes: "bring your pocketbook". You will need it.

After seeing all the hype about their macarons I had to give them a try! We also decided to check out the brunch here. Here's what we got:

- margherita pizza: good pizza, then and crispy but also chewy crust!
- Le pancake: super fluffy and not eggy tasting even though it was a soufflé pancake. It is large and can be shared with 3-4 people. It is quite sweet as well but enjoyed the strawberries and fresh cream!
- truffle fries: basically large chunks of bartered portabella mushrooms, the batter and mushroom don't really congeal well together but the taste was good, esp with the aioli!

The macarons were great! The shell was crispy but chewy. We let it sit out for a while so the cream was too soft but that was on us. Flavors were pretty good!

Overall, I'm glad I gave this place a try. Everything was good, but a bit pricey. Probably wouldn't come here often just bc nothing was super unique but the quality of everything was good!

I've been here twice now and both times I had a decent experience. They started us off with complimentary bread and it was solid. We ordered the Bianco pizza to share as a table and it was definitely the best thing we got there. It's a white sauce pizza with lots of ricotta and was super creamy. After dinner, we walked over to their pastries section and got an assortment of their macrons which were really good. I would recommend trying at least 1 or 2 if you go.

Overall, Bottega Louis had a really nice ambience which is perfect for a date night or event. The staff were all great and the food was good too. While it isn't cheap, I don't think the food is as expensive as other Italian restaurants in the area.

Alex N.
Elite 26
Irvine, CA
15 Brunch reviews
May 15, 2023
5 photos
I used to come here a lot for their chocolate bars, but never really dined here until recently.

We got garage parking in the parking structure across Grand Ave. I believe it's $7 all day, at least on the weekend. The interior is very bright and definitely has an upscale feel.

We had a decent sized group so we ordered multiple items on the weekend brunch menu:
- French toast: the toast had a soft interior and the fruit was fresh. Other than that, just your standard French toast.
- Lobster hash: the lobster tasted really good and the sauce was not bad either
- Portobello fries: really good and pairs perfectly with the aioli sauce. You might want to eat this one quickly or they might get stuck together
- Calamari fritti: good crisp. Also basically just standard calamari
- Croque madame: tasted like an ordinary sandwich.
- Calabrese pizza: each bite has a very fresh taste and also was a bit with the honey
- Tartufo pizza: definitely recommend this one. You can smell the truffle on the melted cheese and you can certainly taste it as well. The egg garnished on the pizza is also nice and adds a nice color to it. My only complaint about this one is the crust is a bit chewy and could be fluffier in a sense.

We also got two cocktails: Juicy and Bellini. Both were nice and sweet, but I would say the Juicy tasted slightly better for us.

Overall, food is a bit on the pricey side, but the quality is pretty much there. Service and ambiance add more value to justify the price too.

Everywhere I looked online says hours are until 12am, but it turns out that the dessert counter closes at 10pm. It was now 10:18pm. We were so sad. While talking to the guy who was closing up the desert counter, he mentioned that we could walk over to the bar and purchase a variety box of random macarons, a blind box, per se. Judy C.
Elite 26
All-Star
Honolulu, HI
56 Brunch reviews
Apr 18, 2022
10 photos
After getting an email from Yelp CM, RE: top 50 most reviewed restaurant and eateries on Yelp. I Had Bottega Louie bookmarked and many others on the list and it was perfect since I was going to Orange County for the weekend. Over 17,000 + reviews and #1 on the list, must visit for me. I was excited, and asked my wonderful hubby the Uber driver to take me. I even gave up my favorite donut spot out at Newport for Bottega. Actually I cheated and had a Krispy Kreme donut along the way.

Important first time info. for newbies like me. No reservations, walk ins only, valet parking only, and the long line in front is not for the restaurant, it is for the bakery ( I was in the wrong line but it worked out as I wanted to get desserts while the other half went to get a table) Expect a long wait and also to show proof of vaccination as we had to show ours during the month of March. Also expect noise from the busy crowd, if you want quiet this is not a place for you.

Bottega Louie is super nice, huge restaurant, a gourmet market, patisserie and cafe. Located in Downtown Los Angeles. W/only one hour on the meter we were limited on time. My hubby did not want to walk back to car to feed the meter and walk back, ( our mistake, next time we will have to plan better) We had to rush and ended up only getting and sharing the lobster hash $29., which was recommended by our server. The lobster hash was amazingly delicious, I loved how the entree was put together. The hash was nice and crispy, loved popping the egg yolk, and the sauce was so good with complimentary bread, I also loved eating the bread with the egg yolk and I saved the the lobster, the best for last.

For desserts, I got the 6 piece macaroon in a heart shaped box ($20.) and original beignets to go. The flavors of macaroon all sound so good and it was hard to choose. The beignets, my opinion taste more like a malasada (Portuguese fried dough) because of the sugar, did not come with the powdered sugar. I didn't know there were more pastries on the other end, wanted to try the Kouign but didn't want to wait in line. next time.

All in all, we had a great first time experience at the most reviewed restaurant on Yelp and I plan to be back again soon. This time I have plans for more lobster hash and def. try the lunch items. We will be back soon, Bottega's already on my list for my upcoming trip.
Totally recommend, just be prepared since it is a very popular restaurant.

We ended with the chicken parm and it was not up to the others in terms of tastes and quality.

The night before we came for dessert and had the soufflé. It was wonderful, fantastic texture, the right sweetness, made to perfection. Wow.

The consistency of good quality and tastes makes this a must stop for anyone in LA.
